  â˜…â˜…â˜…Â½     Watched by kaihoneck  29 Oct 2024   
The Wild Robot soars to emotional highs, but crash-landed in the end.
The first 2/3rds of the film was a 3 act structure and self-contained story. It was moving, funny, heart-wrenching, sentimental, and fantastic. 5 stars for this
The last 3rd of the movie is an entirely different 3-act structure that is a messy action movie with several separate plot threads. 2 stars for the ending.
Still, I liked it quite a bit.
  
  â˜…â˜…â˜…â˜…Â½      Watched by StephenSheehy  26 Oct 2024   
This was a wonderful surprise. I laughed a lot, I cried even more, I was in awe of it's beautiful imagery and I bopped to the soundtrack. Has important messages and life lessons without ever being preachy. The voice cast is starry but they are all well cast and actually add dimensions to their characters. Influences of Wall-E, The Jungle Book, The Iron Giant, Silent Running, Wolfwalkers, Studio Ghibli, the paintings of Monet and Winnie The Pooh to name but a few. All of which are great places to draw inspiration from. Easily one of the best original animated movies from a Western Studio in years.

  â˜…â˜…â˜…     Watched by Rupert Cole  27 Oct 2024
